Hi Fred,

My name is Mitch Popa. I wrote you a couple years ago about a video project I was producing about Costa Rica's ecotourism industry. I hope you don't mind me contacting you again regarding my next round of production.

I've started a website called sustainabletv.org. My main goal is to help market small-scale hotels in central America and specifically Costa Rica. One of the categories is ecotourism. That is the category I am focusing on.

This summer, mid-June to mid-August, we will be back in Costa Rica producing segments on small-scale hotels, ecolodges and rural-community tourism projects.

You can see the quality of our work at sustainabletv.org. Click on the 'watch stv' button, that will take you to the ecotourism category. Drag the mouse over any of the thumbnails at the bottom to view the lodge segments and other documentaries we produced on the last round.

There is a one time fee of $900 to be included plus 3 days of accommodations for a crew of 4 people. In the past we've tried to do the production over two days but because of rain and other unpredictables, it's easiest if we plan for 3 days to make sure we get the video we need to produce the product you deserve.

In return for your investment, your video segment will be featured on sustainabletv.org indefinitely. You are also welcome and encouraged to use the video as part of your internal marketing efforts (Rancho Leona's website, youtube, facebook etc.) An open-ended invitation to send us video or photo updates showing improvements, new construction, unique wildlife sightings etc. Complete access to all our video stills that we shoot during our stay. Rancho Leona will be the subject of our video blog while we are on property. The purpose for the blog is to inform those who are following our trip about where we are and what we are doing. Those segments will remain in archives and available for viewing. Sustainabletrip.org will also be promoting the production on their website and their twitter and facebook accounts.

My goal is for sustainabletv.org to serve as an effective arm of your marketing efforts. I'm driving this site towards the ever-expanding market of 'the nature traveler'. My success lies in getting people to watch the segment so you can know that I'll be doing everything I can to get those researching Costa Rica to find sustainabletv.org

If stv looks like something you want to be a part of, I look forward to meeting and working with you. If you have any questions or concerns, please don't hesitate to contact me.

Best Regards,
